< text>
Great friendly little bar on base. They have free pizza during "happy hour". I my case it was not free. It was the first place I found after arriving on a Space A flight and checking into my room. Don't be a rookie like me and walk in with a baseball cap (hat) or you will hear cheers and a bell ring. Next thing you know your buying a round for the bar. Thankfully, when I entered only four people where at the bar. The round was $32.00 with tip. Four new friends, great conversation and several slices of pizza (to try to make up for the loss).

They also have rules against putting a cell phone on the bar (almost got me on that one also) & touching any of the model aircraft hanging from the ceiling so be careful.

Hey, I am retired Air Force what do I know about crazy Navy rules. It was all good.<//text>

< review>
Before I get into my comment, let me state that I have event planning and catering experience. I really like your venue and there is great potential for your future success! Hopefully this will help...
I attended a wedding on Friday May 4th, 2018. I'm always open to new venues and was looking forward to the experience. It is unfortunate the fire burned most of your property, and rebuilding is a tremendous expense.... BUT that doesn't excuse a lack of awareness from your staff!
The ceremony started at 4pm in the blazing sun, so we sat in the back row with our umbrella not to obstruct anyones view. Unfortunately we could NOT hear a word the bride and groom had to say, BUT we heard EVERY word of the employees setting up food and drink down behind us, as well as them throwing stuff around! PLEASE be aware of this factor... Sound travels up!
When my friends and I wanted to go down to the petting area, it was closed!! No sign or anyone to tell us how long the petting area was open. It was disappointing!
No one let us know the buffet was open and no one was there to tell us what was being offered.
Your bartenders were on their game and didn't skip a beat, but there were several woman who mostly sat around and visibly could careless!
Obviously, I am not aware of your agreement with the bride and groom, but nevertheless, this is the time to REALLY step it up to entice future business.
Hope this helps and Good Luck in the future!<//review>

<Pics>None<//Pics><user_name>alice grazziani</user_name>< Date>

<user_id>116776974523005701840< /user_id>< text>
My son's wedding was held on 6/22/18. The ceremony was at 5:30 and the party went on until very late into the night.
Ranch staff is amazing!! I can't say enough about how accommodating they were to us prior to the wedding and the day of.

Food: A fun food truck or trucks would be ideal. The ranch currently does not have anywhere to cook or prepare foods. Caterers hired must have outdoor kitchen that they bring with them and they should be highly experienced in outdoor cooking with no sink, cooking source or refrigeration. This is very important for you to note and find solutions to safe eating for your guests. I wish I could have convinced my son to do this but they were set to go with a caterer who did not have this experience.

Venue:  it's simply beautiful. Very rustic and open. The lighting at night is very nice and the tree's light up, its magical.
The owners just added a vineyard. I was disappointed that nothing was growing on it yet, but in a few months it is going to be amazing. They seem to be constantly working on improvements. They planted flower boxes going down the bride path and it would have been nice if they planted white flowers or lavender would be best so it ties with most weddings.
The seat area where guest sit need sails or something to shade guest. They set up four umbrellas and guest tried squeezing under them. I recommend bride party purchase nice shade umbrellas for all guests until this is resolved or trees grow.

Weather: it gets hot, it was 90 degrees and I was very concerned about the flowers. Florist need to know that the flowers of set up to early, will be in full sun.
It starts to cool down in the evening and you will need a light sweater. My son rented 6 heaters which I felt were unnecessary. They were not used and it was a waste of money. There is also a firepit and lots of folks hung out there and made smores.
Do not drink and drive! We provided uber rides to guests and a couple took advantage of it.

Overall it was beautiful.</text>

< Text>
If you consider yourself a foodie, make Ten Ren your first stop on any visit to the San Gabriel Valley.  With multiple locations and a huge menu, Ten Ren is so much more than a boba place!  They offer classic Chinese/Taiwanese snacks, tea-based drinks, alcohol, and even full meals like hot pots and various fried rice dishes. I live on the East Coast, but I hit up Ten Ren on every visit to So Cal.  In fact, I will be going there this evening for my usual fried tofu, tea marinated eggs, and a matcha milk tea.  It‚Äôs so nice, while traveling, to snack on something that hasn‚Äôt been purchased at a convenience store.  Service is always friendly and usually fast to boot.  Love me some Ten Ren!</Text>

< text>
My buddy and I come here a couple times a month for a round of disc golf. Park is usually quite clean, though some trash often accumulates in/around the creeks/moats passing through the course. Overall a nice, relatively flat place to play at. Be careful in the reeds around the water as you might end up wearing a Golden Orbweaver. They're relatively harmless, but if you don't like spiders, they'll definitely give you a start!< /text>
